thub.com/tosdr/tosdr-chrome/pull/7</a><br><br><br>On Sunday, December 1, 20=
13 7:28:37 PM UTC-5, Gabriel Perez wrote:<blockquote class=3D"gmail_quote" =
style=3D"margin: 0;margin-left: 0.8ex;border-left: 1px #ccc solid;padding-l=
eft: 1ex;"><div dir=3D"ltr">Is there any interest on adding a feature that =
allows users to express their dislike/like of a particular terms of service=
? I think if many people voted against (or in favor) of&nbsp; a particular =
terms of it could send a powerful message to the organization hosting the s=
ite. In the screenshot I am proposing these as something to vote on the ove=
rall terms of service. But perhaps it could be something for each particula=
r issue. The implementation for this is fairly easy. The "biggest problem" =
is the backend, which is also really simple, but would require hosting and =
